OBJECT Report 78758 Interne begroting INFRA
{
  OBJECT-PROPERTIES
  {
    Date=;
    Time=;
    Version List=4PS9.00.SMART;
  }
  PROPERTIES
  {
    CaptionML=ENU=Interne begroting IBS;
    OnPreReport=BEGIN

                  CRFilter := "Estimate Line NEW".GETFILTERS;
                  CompInfo.GET;
                  CompInfo.CALCFIELDS(Picture);

                  CLEAR(WarningArr);

                  IF CompressReceiptLines THEN
                    CompressReceiptLinesTxt := 'Receptregels zijn verdicht';

                  TryOutCode := TryOutRelationRec.GetTryOut('',"Estimate Line NEW".GETFILTER("Estimate No."),'','','','','',1);
                  IF TryOutCode <> '' THEN
                    TryOut.GET(TryOutCode);
                    //TryOutQuote.GET(TryOutCode);

                  IF TryOutRelationRec.GetTryOut('',"Estimate Line NEW".GETFILTER("Estimate No."),'','','','','',2) <> '' THEN
                    TryOutQuote.GET(TryOutRelationRec.GetTryOut('',"Estimate Line NEW".GETFILTER("Estimate No."),'','','','','',2));

                  SubEstimateFilter := "Estimate Line NEW".GETFILTER("Sub-Estimate No.");

                  EstimateRec.GET("Estimate Line NEW".GETFILTER("Estimate No."));

                  //IF EstimateRec."Estimate Type" = EstimateRec."Estimate Type"::Sales THEN
                  //  ERROR(Text010, EstimateRec."No.");
                  EstimatePrincipal.SETRANGE("Estimate No.",EstimateRec."No.");
                  IF EstimatePrincipal.FINDFIRST THEN;

                  CLEAR(TempRecipeLine);
                  TempRecipeLine.RESET;
                  TempRecipeLine.DELETEALL;
                END;

    OnPostReport=VAR
                   SummarySheet@1100525003 : Record 11012172;
                   SummarySheetLine@1100525002 : Record 11012171;
                   SummarySheetCode@1100525001 : Code[20];
                   i@1100525000 : Integer;
                 BEGIN

                   IF (DiffNormCounter <> 0) AND (ShowNormSet) THEN BEGIN
                     IF DiffNormCounter = 1 THEN
                       MESSAGE(Text002,DiffNormCounter);
                     IF DiffNormCounter > 1 THEN BEGIN
                       MESSAGE(Text002a,DiffNormCounter);
                     END;
                   END;

                   IF ShowSummarrySheet THEN BEGIN
                     SummarySheet.SETRANGE("Estimate No.",EstimateRec."No.");
                     IF SummarySheet.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
                       IF CONFIRM(Text004,TRUE) THEN BEGIN
                         IF PAGE.RUNMODAL(0,SummarySheet) = ACTION::LookupOK THEN BEGIN
                           SummarySheetCode := SummarySheet.Summary;
                           SummarySheetLine.SETRANGE("Estimate No.",EstimateRec."No.");
                           SummarySheetLine.SETRANGE(Summary,SummarySheetCode);
                           IF SummarySheetLine.FINDSET THEN
                             REPORT.RUNMODAL(72645, TRUE, FALSE, SummarySheetLine);
                          END;
                       END
                     END ELSE
                       MESSAGE(Text003,EstimateRec."No.");
                   END;
                 END;

  }
  DATASET
  {
    { 1100525000;;DataItem;                  ;
               DataItemTable=Table11072072;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Estimate No.,Sub-Estimate No.,Part Group,Part,Line No.);
               OnPreDataItem=VAR
                               lDeptCode@1100525000 : Code[20];
                               Language@1000000000 : Record 8;
                             BEGIN
                               DiffNormCounter := 0;
                               TempRecipeLine.RESET;
                               TempRecipeLine.DELETEALL;
                               LastFieldNo := FIELDNO(Part);

                               CLEAR(NormTxt);
                               IF PrintNorm THEN
                                 NormTxt := 'Norm/ eenheid';

                               CLEAR(HoursTxt);
                               IF PrintHours THEN
                                 HoursTxt := 'Uren Totaal';

                               CLEAR(LaborTxt);
                               IF PrintLabor THEN BEGIN
                                 LaborTxt := 'Arbeid Totaal';
                                 LaborSign := Euro;
                               END;

                               CLEAR(MaterialTxt);
                               IF PrintMaterial THEN BEGIN
                                 MaterialTxt := 'Materiaal Totaal';
                                 MaterialSigntxt := Euro;
                               END;

                               CLEAR(SubcontractTxt);
                               IF PrintSubcontract THEN BEGIN
                                 SubcontractTxt := 'Onderaann. Totaal';
                                 SubContractSign := Euro;
                               END;

                               CLEAR(PlantTxt);
                               IF PrintPlant THEN BEGIN
                                 PlantTxt := 'Materieel Totaal';
                                 PlantSign := Euro;
                               END;

                               CLEAR(TotalTxt);
                               IF PrintTotal THEN BEGIN
                                 TotalTxt := 'Totaal';
                                 TotalSign := Euro;
                               END;

                               CLEAR(BrAmntTxt);
                               IF PrintBrAmnt THEN BEGIN
                                 BrAmntTxt := 'Bruto materiaal/ eenheid';
                                 BrAmntSign := Euro;
                               END;

                               CLEAR(PercDiscTxt);
                               IF PrintPercDisc THEN BEGIN
                                 PercDiscTxt := 'Korting';
                                 PercDiscSign := Perc;
                               END;

                               CLEAR(PriceTxt);
                               IF PrintPrice THEN BEGIN
                                 PriceTxt := 'Netto materiaal/ eenheid';
                                 PriceSign := Euro;
                               END;


                               PrintColumns := PrintNorm OR PrintHours OR PrintLabor OR PrintMaterial OR PrintSubcontract OR
                                               PrintPlant OR PrintTotal;

                               IF PrintColumns THEN
                                 TotalLbl := 'Totaal voor Onderdeel'
                               ELSE
                                 TotalLbl := 'Einde Onderdeel';

                               IF EstimateRec."Rate Group" <> '' THEN
                                 TarievenSet := EstimateRec."Rate Group";
                               IF EstimateRec."Norm Group" <> '' THEN
                                 NormenSet := EstimateRec."Norm Group";
                               IF (EstimateRec."Priority Purch Disc Term Grp 0" = '') AND (EstimateRec."Priority Purch Disc Term Grp 1" = '') THEN
                                 KortingLabel := Text001
                               ELSE
                                 KortingLabel := Text001a;

                               IF (EstimateRec."Priority Purch Disc Term Grp 1" > EstimateRec."Priority Purch Disc Term Grp 0") AND
                                 (EstimateRec."Priority Purch Disc Term Grp 2" > EstimateRec."Priority Purch Disc Term Grp 1") THEN
                                 KortingReeks := EstimateRec."Purch Discount Term Group 2";
                               IF (EstimateRec."Priority Purch Disc Term Grp 1" < EstimateRec."Priority Purch Disc Term Grp 0") AND
                                 (EstimateRec."Priority Purch Disc Term Grp 1" > EstimateRec."Priority Purch Disc Term Grp 0") THEN
                                 KortingReeks := 'Bedrijf';
                               IF (EstimateRec."Priority Purch Disc Term Grp 0" = '') AND (EstimateRec."Priority Purch Disc Term Grp 1" = '') AND
                                 (EstimateRec."Priority Purch Disc Term Grp 2" = '') THEN
                                 KortingReeks := 'Bedrijf';

                               EstimateRec.CALCFIELDS("Name Estimator","Customer Name");

                               DimValRec.SETCURRENTKEY(Code,"Global Dimension No.");
                               DimValRec.SETRANGE(Code,EstimateRec."Global Dimension 1 Code");
                               DimValRec.SETRANGE("Global Dimension No.",1);
                               IF DimValRec.FINDFIRST THEN;
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  lvEstimateLine@1100525006 : Record 11072072;
                                  lvRecipeLine@1100525005 : Record 11072075;
                                  lvEstimateLineRec@1100525004 : Record 11072072;
                                  EstimateLine@1100525003 : Record 11072072;
                                  lSubEst@1100525002 : Record 11072074;
                                  LastOccInt@1100525001 : Integer;
                                  i@1100525000 : Integer;
                                  TempCorrDec@1100525007 : Decimal;
                                BEGIN

                                  IF NOT (CalcB) AND (PrintSummaryBl) THEN BEGIN
                                    GenerateTempLines("Estimate No.");
                                    CalcB := TRUE;
                                  END;

                                  CLEAR(SubOperation);
                                  IF ("Sub Operation Code" <> '') AND (ShowSubProc) THEN BEGIN
                                    SubOperation.GET("Sub Operation Code");
                                  END ELSE
                                    SubOperation.INIT;


                                  IF (TempPartNo <>'') AND (TempPartNo <> Part) THEN BEGIN
                                    CLEAR(TempRecipeLine);
                                    TempRecipeLine.RESET;
                                    TempRecipeLine.DELETEALL;
                                    CountBl := FALSE;
                                  END;

                                  IF ("Line No." <> 0) AND ("Estimate Line NEW"."Norm Group" <> EstimateRec."Norm Group") THEN BEGIN
                                    IF (Quantity <> 0) AND ("Sub Operation Code" <> '') OR (Quantity <> 0) AND ("Norm Group" <> '') THEN
                                      DiffNormCounter := DiffNormCounter + 1;
                                  END;

                                  IF ("Line No." <> 0) AND (ShowNormSet) AND ("Estimate Line NEW"."Norm Group" <> EstimateRec."Norm Group") THEN BEGIN
                                    InsertNormDiffLine("Estimate Line NEW");
                                  END;

                                  IF (CompressReceiptLines) AND NOT (CountBl) THEN BEGIN
                                    lvEstimateLineRec.RESET;
                                    lvEstimateLineRec.SETRANGE("Estimate No.","Estimate No.");
                                    lvEstimateLineRec.SETRANGE("Sub-Estimate No.","Sub-Estimate No.");
                                    lvEstimateLineRec.SETRANGE("Part Group","Part Group");
                                    lvEstimateLineRec.SETRANGE(Part,Part);
                                    lvEstimateLineRec.SETFILTER("Part Quantity",'<>%1',0);
                                    IF lvEstimateLineRec.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
                                      RecCounter := lvEstimateLineRec.COUNT;
                                      TempRecCounter := RecCounter;
                                      CountBl := TRUE;
                                    END;
                                  END;

                                  IF (CompressReceiptLines) AND (CountBl) THEN
                                    RecCounter := RecCounter - 1;

                                  IF CompressReceiptLines THEN BEGIN
                                    lvRecipeLine.INIT;
                                    IF "Estimate Line NEW".Recipe = '' THEN BEGIN
                                      InsertOrModifyTempRecLine(lvRecipeLine,"Estimate Line NEW",Quantity,Quantity) //MMA.n
                                    END ELSE BEGIN
                                      IF Quantity <> 0 THEN BEGIN
                                        lvEstimateLineRec.INIT;
                                        lvRecipeLine.RESET;
                                        lvRecipeLine.SETRANGE("Estimate No.","Estimate No.");
                                        lvRecipeLine.SETRANGE("Sub-Estimate No.","Sub-Estimate No.");
                                        lvRecipeLine.SETRANGE("Estimate Line","Line No.");
                                        lvRecipeLine.SETRANGE("Part Group","Part Group");
                                        lvRecipeLine.SETRANGE(Part,Part);
                                        lvRecipeLine.SETRANGE(Recipe,Recipe);
                                        lvRecipeLine.SETRANGE("Recipe Group","Recipe Group");
                                        IF lvRecipeLine.FINDSET THEN
                                          REPEAT
                                            InsertOrModifyTempRecLine(lvRecipeLine,lvEstimateLineRec,Quantity * lvRecipeLine.Quantity,Quantity); //MMA.n
                                          UNTIL lvRecipeLine.NEXT = 0;
                                      END;
                                    END;
                                  END;

                                  ItemCode := "Item No.";
                                  IF "Basic Item" <> '' THEN
                                    ItemCode := Manufacturer + ' ' + "Basic Item";
                                  IF "Trade Item" <> '' THEN
                                    ItemCode := "Vendor (Trade Item)" + ' ' + "Trade Item";
                                  IF Recipe <> '' THEN
                                    ItemCode := Recipe;

                                  TryOutCode := TryOutRelationRec.GetTryOut('',"Estimate No.",'','','','','',1);
                                  IF TryOutQuoteRec.GET(TryOutCode) THEN;

                                  CALCFIELDS("Quantity Model Exist");

                                  IF (TempPart <> Part) OR (TempSubEstimate <> "Sub-Estimate No.") THEN BEGIN
                                    //TempPart := Part;
                                    HoursTotal[1] := 0;
                                    LaborTotal[1] := 0;
                                    MaterialTotal[1] := 0;
                                    SubcontractTotal[1] := 0;
                                    PlantTotal[1] := 0;
                                    AmountTotal[1] := 0;
                                    GrossAmountTotal[1] := 0; //MMA.n
                                  END;

                                  IF TempSubEstimate <> "Sub-Estimate No." THEN BEGIN
                                    //TempSubEstimate := "Sub-Estimate No.";
                                    HoursTotal[2] := 0;
                                    LaborTotal[2] := 0;
                                    MaterialTotal[2] := 0;
                                    SubcontractTotal[2] := 0;
                                    PlantTotal[2] := 0;
                                    AmountTotal[2] := 0;
                                    GrossAmountTotal[2] := 0; //MMA.n
                                  END;

                                  TempSubEstimate := "Sub-Estimate No."; //0710
                                  TempPart := Part;  //0710



                                  NormDec[1] := 0;
                                  HoursDec[1] := 0;
                                  LaborDec[1] := 0;
                                  MaterialDec[1] := 0;
                                  SubcontractDec[1] := 0;
                                  PlantDec[1] := 0;
                                  TotalDec[1] := 0;
                                  DiscountPercDec := 0;
                                  SurchDec := 0;
                                  //GrossAmountDec := 0; //MMA.o
                                  GrossAmountDec[1] := 0; //MMA.n

                                  PartQuant := "Part Quantity";

                                  IF (PrintSummaryBl) AND ("Rate Code" <> '') AND (Recipe = '') THEN BEGIN
                                    InsertOrModifyRates("Rate Code", Hours, "Labor Cost Amount" * PartQuant);
                                  END;


                                  IF PrintNorm THEN
                                    NormDec[1] := Norm;


                                  IF PrintHours THEN BEGIN
                                    HoursDec[1] := ROUND(Hours * PartQuant,0.01);
                                    HoursTotal[1] += ROUND(Hours * PartQuant,0.01);
                                    HoursTotal[2] += ROUND(Hours * PartQuant,0.01);
                                  END;

                                  IF PrintLabor THEN BEGIN
                                    LaborDec[1] := ("Labor Cost Amount" * PartQuant);
                                    LaborTotal[1] += ("Labor Cost Amount" * PartQuant);
                                    LaborTotal[2] += ("Labor Cost Amount" * PartQuant);
                                  END;

                                  IF PrintMaterial THEN BEGIN
                                    MaterialDec[1] := ("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant);
                                    MaterialTotal[1] += ("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant);
                                    MaterialTotal[2] += ("Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant);
                                  END;

                                  IF PrintSubcontract THEN BEGIN
                                    SubcontractDec[1] := ("Subcontracting Cost Amount" * PartQuant);
                                    SubcontractTotal[1] += ("Subcontracting Cost Amount" * PartQuant);
                                    SubcontractTotal[2] += ("Subcontracting Cost Amount" * PartQuant);
                                  END;

                                  IF PrintPlant THEN BEGIN
                                    PlantDec[1] := ("Plant Cost Amount" * PartQuant);
                                    PlantTotal[1] += ("Plant Cost Amount" * PartQuant);
                                    PlantTotal[2] += ("Plant Cost Amount" * PartQuant);
                                  END;

                                  IF PrintTotal THEN BEGIN
                                    TotalDec[1] := ("Cost Amount" * PartQuant);
                                    AmountTotal[1] += ("Cost Amount" * PartQuant);
                                    AmountTotal[2] += ("Cost Amount" * PartQuant);
                                  END;

                                  IF PrintPrice THEN BEGIN
                                    Price := 0;
                                    IF Quantity <> 0 THEN
                                      Price := "Cost Amount" / Quantity;
                                  END ELSE
                                    "Material Sales Amount" := 0;

                                  //IF PrintPercDisc THEN
                                  //  DiscountPercDec := "Discount %";

                                  IF PrintSurch THEN
                                    SurchDec := "Surcharge %";

                                  IF PrintBrAmnt THEN BEGIN
                                    GrossAmountDec[1] := "Gross Price";
                                    GrossAmountTotal[1] += "Gross Price";
                                    GrossAmountTotal[2] += "Gross Price";
                                  END;
                                  //MMA.en

                                  lvEstimateLineRec.SETRANGE("Estimate No.","Estimate No.");
                                  lvEstimateLineRec.SETRANGE("Sub-Estimate No.","Sub-Estimate No.");
                                  lvEstimateLineRec.SETFILTER("Line Status",'NC');
                                  lvEstimateLineRec.SETFILTER(Quantity,'<>%1',0);
                                  IF lvEstimateLineRec.FINDFIRST THEN
                                    NCBool := TRUE
                                  ELSE
                                    NCBool := FALSE;

                                  //Hoeveelheden onderdeel
                                  IF PartQuant <> 1 THEN
                                    Quantity := Quantity * PartQuant;

                                  CLEAR(DescriptionTxt);
                                  IF "Line Status" <> '' THEN BEGIN
                                    LineStatus := "Line Status";
                                    IF ("Line Status" = 'NC') AND (Quantity <> 0) THEN       //GB.24-03-2010;
                                      DescriptionTxt := STRSUBSTNO('***** BOVENSTAANDE REGEL NIET COMPLEET *****',"Estimate Line NEW".Part);
                                    END ELSE
                                      LineStatus := '';

                                  IF  (DescriptionTxt = '') AND (STRLEN(Description) > 58) THEN BEGIN
                                    FOR i := 45 DOWNTO 1 DO
                                      IF (COPYSTR(Description,i,1) = ' ')  AND (LastOccInt = 0) THEN
                                        LastOccInt := i;
                                    DescriptionTxt := COPYSTR(Description, LastOccInt + 1, STRLEN(Description) - LastOccInt);
                                    IF LastOccInt <> 0 THEN
                                      Description := COPYSTR(Description,1, LastOccInt -1);
                                  END;



                                  TempPartNo := Part;

                                  IF (CompressReceiptLines) AND (RecCounter = 0) THEN BEGIN
                                    PrintLines := TRUE;
                                    CountBl := FALSE;
                                  END;

                                  IF (Quantity = 0) AND ("Unit of Measure" <> '') AND NOT (CompressReceiptLines) AND NOT (PrintZeroLines)
                                    THEN CurrReport.SKIP;

                                  IF STRPOS(TempRecipeLine.Description,'SNIT') <> 0 THEN BEGIN
                                    DiscountPercDec := 0;
                                    GrossAmountDec[1] := 0;
                                    Price := 0;
                                  END;


                                  //FROM SECTION
                                  ShowELO2 := (CRFilter <> '');

                                  IF TempEstim <> "Estimate No." THEN BEGIN
                                    TempEstim := "Estimate No.";
                                    CurrReport.PAGENO := 1;
                                  END;

                                  EstimateRec.CALCFIELDS("Customer Name", "Contact Name");
                                  EstimatePrincipal.CALCFIELDS(Name);

                                  IF NOT TryOutQteDateBl THEN
                                    DateTxt := STRSUBSTNO('%1',FORMAT(AlternativeDate))
                                  ELSE BEGIN
                                    DateTxt := STRSUBSTNO('%1',FORMAT(TryOutQuote."Register Date"));
                                  END;


                                  IF PrintLineStatus THEN
                                    LineStatusTxt := "Line Status"
                                  ELSE
                                    LineStatusTxt := '';

                                  IF Recipe <>'' THEN
                                    ReceiptID := 'R'
                                  ELSE
                                    ReceiptID := '';

                                  IF "Surcharge %" <> 0 THEN
                                    PercLabelSnit := Perc
                                  ELSE
                                    PercLabelSnit := '';

                                  //CurrReport.SHOWOUTPUT(NOT CompressReceiptLines);
                                  //CurrReport.SHOWOUTPUT((PrintZeroLines) AND (NOT CompressReceiptLines) OR
                                  //  (NOT PrintZeroLines) AND (Quantity <> 0) AND (NOT CompressReceiptLines));

                                  ShowELO9 := TRUE;
                                  IF (NOT PrintZeroLines) THEN BEGIN
                                    ShowELO9 := (FALSE);
                                    IF  (LaborDec[1] = 0) AND (GrossAmountDec[1] = 0) AND ("Material Sales Amount" = 0) AND (Quantity = 0) AND ("Unit of Measure" = '') THEN
                                      ShowELO9 := (TRUE);
                                    IF (LaborDec[1] <> 0) OR (GrossAmountDec[1] <> 0) OR ("Material Sales Amount" <> 0) OR (Quantity <> 0)  THEN
                                      ShowELO9 := (TRUE);
                                  END;

                                  IF (PrintZeroLines) THEN BEGIN
                                  END;

                                  IF CompressReceiptLines THEN
                                      ShowELO9 := (FALSE);

                                  ShowELO10 := ((NOT CompressReceiptLines) AND (DescriptionTxt <>''));
                                  ShowELO11 := ((ShowSubProc) AND (SubOperation.Description <> '') AND NOT (CompressReceiptLines));

                                  CLEAR(CorrFactPartText);
                                  CheckCorrFactPart("Estimate No.","Sub-Estimate No.","Part Group",Part);
                                  //MMA.sn
                                  CLEAR(CorrFactText);
                                  CheckCorrFactSubEst("Estimate No.","Sub-Estimate No.",FALSE);
                                  //MMA.en
                                  ShowELO14 := (NCBool);

                                  ShowELO15 := (CorrFactPartText <> '');

                                  //CorrDec := -1 * (HoursTotal[1] - (AdjFactorHours * HoursTotal[1])); //MMA.o
                                  //MMA.sn
                                  CorrDec := 0;
                                  IF (AdjFactorHours <> 0) THEN
                                    CorrDec := HoursTotal[1] - (HoursTotal[1]/AdjFactorHours);
                                  //MMA.en

                                  IF ShowELO15 THEN BEGIN
                                    CorrCounter := CorrCounter + 1;
                                    CorrPartArr[CorrCounter] := CorrDec;
                                    PartArr[CorrCounter] := Part;
                                  END;



                                  TempCorrDec := HoursTotal[1] + -(CorrDec);
                                  CorrDec := 0;

                                  IF (AdjFactorHoursFact <> 0) THEN BEGIN
                                    CorrDec := TempCorrDec - (TempCorrDec / AdjFactorHoursFact);
                                  END;

                                   ShowELO16 := (CorrFactText <> '') AND (CorrDec <> 0);

                                  CLEAR(CorrFactText);
                                  CheckCorrFactSubEst("Estimate No.","Sub-Estimate No.",TRUE);

                                  ShowELO18 := (CorrFactText <> '');


                                  //TempCorrDec := HoursTotal[2] + -(CorrDec);
                                  //CorrDec := 0;

                                  //IF (AdjFactorHoursFact <> 0) THEN BEGIN
                                  //  CorrDec := TempCorrDec - (TempCorrDec / AdjFactorHoursFact);
                                  //END;

                                  //CorrDec := 0;
                                  //IF (AdjFactorHoursFact <> 0) THEN
                                  //  CorrDec := HoursTotal[2] - (HoursTotal[2]/AdjFactorHoursFact);

                                  IF CorrDec = 0 THEN
                                    IF (AdjFactorHoursFact <> 0) THEN
                                      CorrDec := HoursTotal[2] - (HoursTotal[2]/AdjFactorHoursFact);

                                  countrec :=0;
                                END;

               ReqFilterFields=Estimate No.,Sub-Estimate No.,Part Group,Part }

    { 1100525002;1;DataItem;                 ;
               DataItemTable=Table11072075;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Estimate No.,Sub-Estimate No.,Part Group,Part,Estimate Line,Recipe Group,Recipe,Line No.);
               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  lvEstLineRec@1100525003 : Record 11072072;
                                  Quant@1100525002 : Decimal;
                                  lvEstLine@1100525001 : Record 11072072;
                                  SubEstPart@1100525000 : Record 11072073;
                                BEGIN

                                  IF ("Line No." <> 0) AND (ShowNormSet) AND ("Norm Group" <> EstimateRec."Norm Group") THEN BEGIN
                                    InsertNormDiffRecLine("Estimate Recipe Line");
                                  END;

                                  IF ("Line No." <> 0) AND ("Norm Group" <> EstimateRec."Norm Group") THEN BEGIN
                                    IF (Quantity <> 0) AND ("Sub Operation Code" <> '') OR
                                    (Quantity <> 0) AND ("Norm Group" <> '') THEN
                                      DiffNormCounter := DiffNormCounter + 1;
                                  END;

                                  SubEstPart.GET("Estimate No.","Sub-Estimate No.","Part Group",Part);

                                  IF CompressReceiptLines THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;

                                  CLEAR(SubOperation);
                                  IF ("Sub Operation Code" <> '') AND (ShowSubProcReceipt) AND NOT (CompressReceiptLines) THEN BEGIN
                                    SubOperation.GET("Sub Operation Code");
                                  END ELSE
                                    SubOperation.INIT;

                                  lvEstLineRec.GET("Estimate No.", "Sub-Estimate No.", "Part Group", Part, "Estimate Line");
                                  Quantity := Quantity * lvEstLineRec.Quantity;
                                  Hours := Hours * lvEstLineRec.Quantity;
                                  "Cost Amount" := "Cost Amount" * lvEstLineRec.Quantity;

                                  ItemCode := "Item No.";
                                  IF "Basic Item" <> '' THEN
                                    ItemCode := Manufacturer + ' ' + "Basic Item";
                                  IF "Trade Item" <> '' THEN
                                    ItemCode := "Vendor (Trade Item)" + ' ' + "Trade Item";

                                  NormDec[2] := 0;
                                  HoursDec[2] := 0;
                                  LaborDec[2] := 0;
                                  MaterialDec[2] := 0;
                                  MatAmntDec := 0;
                                  SubcontractDec[2] := 0;
                                  PlantDec[2] := 0;
                                  TotalDec[2] := 0;
                                  GrossAmountDec[2] := 0;
                                  PartQuant := lvEstLineRec."Part Quantity";


                                  IF PrintNorm THEN
                                    NormDec[2] := Norm;

                                  IF PrintHours THEN
                                      HoursDec[2] := ROUND(Hours * PartQuant,0.01);

                                  IF PrintLabor THEN
                                      LaborDec[2] := "Labor Cost Amount" * lvEstLineRec.Quantity * PartQuant;

                                  IF PrintMaterial THEN
                                    //MaterialDec[2] := "Material Amount" * lvEstLineRec.Quantity * PartQuant; //o 26-10-2010
                                    //MaterialDec[2] := "Material Price" * lvEstLineRec.Quantity * PartQuant;
                                    MaterialDec[2] := "Material Sales Amount" * Quantity;

                                  IF PrintSubcontract THEN
                                      SubcontractDec[2] := "Subcontracting Cost Amount" * lvEstLineRec.Quantity * PartQuant;

                                  IF PrintPlant THEN
                                      PlantDec[2] := "Plant Cost Amount" * lvEstLineRec.Quantity * PartQuant;

                                  IF PrintTotal THEN
                                      TotalDec[2] := "Cost Amount" * PartQuant;

                                  //MMA.sn
                                  IF PrintBrAmnt THEN
                                    GrossAmountDec[2] := "Gross Price";
                                  //MMA.en

                                  MatAmntDec := "Material Sales Amount";

                                  IF (PrintSummaryBl) AND ("Rate Code" <> '') THEN BEGIN
                                    InsertOrModifyRates("Rate Code", Hours, ("Labor Cost Amount" * lvEstLineRec.Quantity * PartQuant));
                                  END;


                                  IF PartQuant <> 1 THEN
                                    Quantity := Quantity  * PartQuant;

                                  //IF NOT PrintPercDisc THEN
                                  //  "Estimate Recipe Line"."Discount %" := 0;

                                  CLEAR(DescriptionTxt);
                                  IF "Line Status" <> '' THEN BEGIN
                                    LineStatus := "Line Status";
                                    IF ("Line Status" = 'NC') AND (Quantity <> 0) THEN       //GB.24-03-2010;
                                      DescriptionTxt := STRSUBSTNO('***** BOVENSTAANDE REGEL NIET COMPLEET *****');
                                    END ELSE
                                      LineStatus := '';

                                  IF (Quantity = 0) AND ("Unit of Measure" <> '') AND NOT (CompressReceiptLines) AND NOT (PrintZeroRecipeLines)
                                    THEN CurrReport.SKIP;

                                  IF STRPOS(TempRecipeLine.Description,'SNIT') <> 0 THEN BEGIN
                                    DiscountPercDec := 0;
                                    GrossAmountDec[2] := 0;
                                    Price := 0;
                                    Quantity := 0.001;
                                  END;

                                  //FROM SECTION
                                  ShowRLO1 := (PrintRecipeLines);

                                  ShowRLO2 := ((PrintRecipeLines AND PrintZeroRecipeLines) OR
                                                        (PrintRecipeLines AND (NOT PrintZeroLines) AND (Quantity <> 0) AND NOT (CompressReceiptLines)));

                                  IF PrintLineStatus THEN
                                    LineStatusTxt := "Line Status"
                                  ELSE
                                    LineStatusTxt := '';


                                  IF "Surcharge %" <> 0 THEN
                                    PercLabelSnit := Perc
                                  ELSE
                                    PercLabelSnit := '';

                                  ShowRLO3 := (PrintRecipeLines AND (DescriptionTxt <> ''));
                                  ShowRLO4 := ((SubOperation.Description <> '') AND NOT (CompressReceiptLines) AND (ShowSubProcReceipt));
                                  ShowRLO5 := (PrintRecipeLines);

                                  countrec +=1;
                                  IF countrec > 1 THEN
                                  CLEAR(CompInfo.Picture)
                                END;

               DataItemLink=Estimate No.=FIELD(Estimate No.),
                            Sub-Estimate No.=FIELD(Sub-Estimate No.),
                            Part Group=FIELD(Part Group),
                            Part=FIELD(Part),
                            Recipe Group=FIELD(Recipe Group),
                            Recipe=FIELD(Recipe),
                            Estimate Line=FIELD(Line No.) }

    { 1100525003;1;DataItem;ComprRecipeLines ;
               DataItemTable=Table2000000026;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Number);
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN

                               TempRecCounter := TempRecCounter - 1;
                               TempRecipeLine.RESET;

                               SETRANGE(Number,1,TempRecipeLine.COUNT)
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  lvEstLineRec@1100525001 : Record 11072072;
                                  SubEstPart@1100525000 : Record 11072073;
                                BEGIN

                                  IF Number = 1 THEN
                                    TempRecipeLine.FINDFIRST
                                  ELSE
                                    TempRecipeLine.NEXT;

                                  IF (TempRecipeLine."Sub Operation Code" <> '') AND (ShowSubProc) AND (CompressReceiptLines) THEN BEGIN
                                    SubOperation.GET(TempRecipeLine."Sub Operation Code");
                                  END ELSE
                                    SubOperation.INIT;

                                  //SubEstPart.GET(TempRecipeLine."Estimate No.",TempRecipeLine."Sub-Estimate No.",TempRecipeLine."Part Group",
                                  //              TempRecipeLine.Part);

                                  lvEstLineRec.GET(TempRecipeLine."Estimate No.", TempRecipeLine."Sub-Estimate No.",
                                    TempRecipeLine."Part Group", TempRecipeLine.Part, TempRecipeLine."Estimate Line");

                                  ItemCode := TempRecipeLine."Item No.";
                                  IF TempRecipeLine."Basic Item" <> '' THEN
                                    ItemCode := TempRecipeLine.Manufacturer + ' ' + TempRecipeLine."Basic Item";
                                  IF TempRecipeLine."Trade Item" <> '' THEN
                                    ItemCode := TempRecipeLine."Vendor (Trade Item)" + ' ' + TempRecipeLine."Trade Item";

                                  NormDec[2] := 0;
                                  HoursDec[2] := 0;
                                  LaborDec[2] := 0;
                                  MaterialDec[2] := 0;
                                  SubcontractDec[2] := 0;
                                  PlantDec[2] := 0;
                                  TotalDec[2] := 0;
                                  GrossAmountDec[2] := 0;
                                  PartQuant := lvEstLineRec."Part Quantity";


                                  IF PrintNorm THEN
                                    NormDec[2] := TempRecipeLine.Norm;

                                  IF PrintHours THEN
                                    HoursDec[2] := ROUND(TempRecipeLine.Hours * PartQuant,0.01);

                                  IF PrintLabor THEN
                                    LaborDec[2] := TempRecipeLine."Labor Cost Amount" * PartQuant;

                                  IF PrintMaterial THEN
                                    MaterialDec[2] := TempRecipeLine."Material Cost Amount" * PartQuant;

                                  IF PrintSubcontract THEN
                                    SubcontractDec[2] := TempRecipeLine."Subcontracting Cost Amount" * PartQuant;

                                  IF PrintPlant THEN
                                    PlantDec[2] := TempRecipeLine."Plant Cost Amount" * PartQuant;

                                  IF PrintTotal THEN
                                    TotalDec[2] := TempRecipeLine."Cost Amount" * PartQuant;

                                  IF PrintBrAmnt THEN
                                    GrossAmountDec[2] := TempRecipeLine."Gross Price"; //MMA.n

                                  MatAmntDec := TempRecipeLine."Material Sales Amount";

                                  IF PartQuant <> 1 THEN
                                    TempRecipeLine.Quantity := TempRecipeLine.Quantity * PartQuant;

                                  CLEAR(DescriptionTxt);
                                  IF TempRecipeLine."Line Status" <> '' THEN BEGIN
                                    LineStatus := TempRecipeLine."Line Status";
                                    IF (TempRecipeLine."Line Status" = 'NC') AND (TempRecipeLine.Quantity <> 0) THEN       //GB.24-03-2010;
                                      DescriptionTxt := STRSUBSTNO('***** BOVENSTAANDE REGEL NIET COMPLEET *****');
                                    END ELSE
                                      LineStatus := '';

                                  IF (TempRecipeLine.Quantity = 0) AND (TempRecipeLine."Unit of Measure" <> '') AND NOT (PrintZeroLines)
                                    THEN CurrReport.SKIP;

                                  IF STRPOS(TempRecipeLine.Description,'SNIT') <> 0 THEN BEGIN
                                    DiscountPercDec := 0;
                                    GrossAmountDec[2] := 0;
                                    Price := 0;
                                    TempRecipeLine.Quantity := 0.001;
                                  END;

                                  //FROM SECTION

                                  ShowCRL1 := ((CompressReceiptLines) AND (TempRecCounter = 0));

                                  IF PrintLineStatus THEN
                                    LineStatusTxt := TempRecipeLine."Line Status"
                                  ELSE
                                    LineStatusTxt := '';

                                  ShowCRL2 := ((CompressReceiptLines) AND (TempRecCounter = 0) AND (DescriptionTxt <> ''));


                                  ShowCRL3 := ((CompressReceiptLines) AND (ShowSubProc)
                                    AND (SubOperation.Description <> '') AND (TempRecCounter = 0));
                                END;
                                 }

               DataItemTable=Table2000000026;

                                 TempSubEstimateRec.SETFILTER("Sub-Estimate No.",SubEstimateFilter);

                               CurrReport.CREATETOTALS(TempSubEstimateRec.Hours, TempSubEstimateRec."Material Amount",

                                  IF PrintSubcontract THEN
                                     TempSubEstimateRec.CALCFIELDS("Subcontracting Amount");

                                     TempSubEstimateRec.CALCFIELDS("Plant Amount");


                                  //FROM SECTION

                                  //Samenvatting, Footer (6) - OnPreSection()
                                  CALCsumm;

                                  IF SpecMatDec[7] <> 0 THEN BEGIN
                                    SpecMatSignTxt7 := SpecMatTxt;
                                    SpecMatLab7 := SpecMatLab7Txt;
                                  END;
                                END;
                                 }

                               TempSubEstimatePartRec.SETRANGE("Sub-Estimate No.", TempSubEstimateRec."Sub-Estimate No.");

                               SETRANGE(Number,1,TempSubEstimatePartRec.COUNT);

                               CurrReport.CREATETOTALS(TempSubEstimatePartRec."Hours Part", TempSubEstimatePartRec."Material Part",
                               TempSubEstimatePartRec."Subcontracting Part", TempSubEstimatePartRec."Plant Part");

                               IF (TempSubEstimatePartRec.COUNT = 0) THEN
                                 CurrReport.BREAK;
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN

                                  IF Number = 1 THEN
                                    TempSubEstimatePartRec.FINDFIRST
                                  ELSE
                                    TempSubEstimatePartRec.NEXT;

                                  IF PrintHours THEN
                                    TempSubEstimatePartRec.CALCFIELDS("Hours Part");
                                  IF PrintMaterial THEN
                                     TempSubEstimatePartRec.CALCFIELDS("Material Part");
                                  IF PrintSubcontract THEN
                                     TempSubEstimatePartRec.CALCFIELDS("Subcontracting Part");
                                  IF PrintPlant THEN
                                     TempSubEstimatePartRec.CALCFIELDS("Plant Part");


                                  IF Number > 1 THEN BEGIN
                                  TempSubEstimateRec.Hours := 0;
                                  TempSubEstimateRec."Material Amount" := 0;
                                  TempSubEstimateRec."Subcontracting Amount" := 0;
                                  TempSubEstimateRec."Plant Amount" := 0;
                                  END;

                                  //FROM SECTION

                                  ShowSamPart1 := TRUE;
                                  IF NOT PrintZeroLines THEN BEGIN
                                    IF (TempSubEstimatePartRec."Hours Part" = 0) AND
                                      (TempSubEstimatePartRec."Material Part" = 0) AND
                                      (TempSubEstimatePartRec."Subcontracting Part" = 0) AND
                                      (TempSubEstimatePartRec."Plant Part" = 0) THEN
                                      ShowSamPart1 := (FALSE);
                                  END;

                                  IF NOT PrintPartsBySummaryBl THEN
                                    ShowSamPart1 := (FALSE);


                                  IF Number > 1 THEN
                                  CLEAR(CompInfo.Picture)
                                END;

    PROCEDURE InsertOrModifyTempRecLine@1000000017(RecipeLine@1000000000 : Record 11072075;EstLine@1000000001 : Record 11072072;MultiplyQty@1100525000 : Decimal;EstLineQuantity@1000000002 : Decimal);
    BEGIN
      IF RecipeLine."Estimate No." <> '' THEN BEGIN
        TempRecipeLine.RESET;
        TempRecipeLine.SETRANGE("Sub Operation Code",RecipeLine."Sub Operation Code");
        TempRecipeLine.SETRANGE("Trade Item",RecipeLine."Trade Item");
        TempRecipeLine.SETRANGE("Unit of Measure",RecipeLine."Unit of Measure");
        TempRecipeLine.SETRANGE("Line Status",RecipeLine."Line Status");
        TempRecipeLine.SETRANGE("Sub-Estimate No.", RecipeLine."Sub-Estimate No.");
        TempRecipeLine.SETRANGE("Part Group", RecipeLine."Part Group");
        TempRecipeLine.SETRANGE(Part, RecipeLine.Part);
        TempRecipeLine.SETRANGE(Description,RecipeLine.Description);
        IF TempRecipeLine.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
          TempRecipeLine.Quantity := TempRecipeLine.Quantity + (RecipeLine.Quantity * EstLineQuantity); // MultiplyQty); 16092001.GB
          TempRecipeLine."Material Cost Amount" := TempRecipeLine."Material Cost Amount" + (RecipeLine."Material Cost Amount" * EstLineQuantity);
          TempRecipeLine."Subcontracting Cost Amount" := TempRecipeLine."Subcontracting Cost Amount" +
            (RecipeLine."Subcontracting Cost Amount" * EstLineQuantity);
          TempRecipeLine."Labor Cost Amount" := TempRecipeLine."Labor Cost Amount" + (RecipeLine."Labor Cost Amount" * EstLineQuantity);
          TempRecipeLine."Plant Cost Amount" := TempRecipeLine."Plant Cost Amount" + (RecipeLine."Plant Cost Amount" * EstLineQuantity);
          TempRecipeLine.Hours := TempRecipeLine.Hours + (RecipeLine.Hours * EstLineQuantity);
          TempRecipeLine."Cost Amount" := TempRecipeLine."Cost Amount" + RecipeLine."Cost Amount";
          TempRecipeLine.MODIFY;
        END ELSE
          CreateTempRecipeLine(RecipeLine, EstLineQuantity, EstLineQuantity); //MMA.n
      END ELSE BEGIN
        TempRecipeLine.RESET;
        TempRecipeLine.SETRANGE("Sub Operation Code",EstLine."Sub Operation Code");
        TempRecipeLine.SETRANGE("Trade Item",EstLine."Trade Item");
        TempRecipeLine.SETRANGE("Unit of Measure",EstLine."Unit of Measure");
        TempRecipeLine.SETRANGE("Line Status",EstLine."Line Status");
        TempRecipeLine.SETRANGE("Sub-Estimate No.", EstLine."Sub-Estimate No.");
        TempRecipeLine.SETRANGE("Part Group", EstLine."Part Group");
        TempRecipeLine.SETRANGE(Part, EstLine.Part);
        TempRecipeLine.SETRANGE(Description,EstLine.Description);
        IF TempRecipeLine.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
          TempRecipeLine.Quantity := TempRecipeLine.Quantity + EstLine.Quantity;
          TempRecipeLine."Material Cost Amount" := TempRecipeLine."Material Cost Amount" + EstLine."Material Cost Amount";
          TempRecipeLine."Subcontracting Cost Amount" := TempRecipeLine."Subcontracting Cost Amount" + EstLine."Subcontracting Cost Amount";
          TempRecipeLine."Labor Cost Amount" := TempRecipeLine."Labor Cost Amount" + EstLine."Labor Cost Amount";
          TempRecipeLine."Plant Cost Amount" := TempRecipeLine."Plant Cost Amount" + EstLine."Plant Cost Amount";
          TempRecipeLine.Hours := TempRecipeLine.Hours + EstLine.Hours;
          //TempRecipeLine."Gross Price" := TempRecipeLine."Gross Price" + EstLine."Gross Price";
          //TempRecipeLine."Material Price" := TempRecipeLine."Material Price" + EstLine."Material Price";
          //TempRecipeLine."Subcontracting Price" := TempRecipeLine."Subcontracting Price" + EstLine."Subcontracting Price";
          TempRecipeLine."Cost Amount":= TempRecipeLine."Cost Amount"+ EstLine."Cost Amount";
          TempRecipeLine.MODIFY;
        END ELSE
          CreateTempEstLine(EstLine);
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE CreateTempRecipeLine@1000000022(RecipeLine@1000000000 : Record 11072075;MultiplyQty@1100525000 : Decimal;Qty@1000000001 : Decimal);
    BEGIN
      BEGIN //MMA.n
        TempRecipeLine.INIT;
        TempRecipeLine.COPY(RecipeLine);
        TempRecipeLine.Quantity := (TempRecipeLine.Quantity * Qty); // MultiplyQty); 16092001.GB
        TempRecipeLine."Cost Amount":= (RecipeLine."Cost Amount"* MultiplyQty);
        TempRecipeLine."Labor Cost Amount" := RecipeLine."Labor Cost Amount" * MultiplyQty;
        TempRecipeLine."Material Cost Amount" := RecipeLine."Material Cost Amount" * MultiplyQty;
        TempRecipeLine."Subcontracting Cost Amount" := RecipeLine."Subcontracting Cost Amount" * MultiplyQty;
        TempRecipeLine."Plant Cost Amount" := RecipeLine."Plant Cost Amount" * MultiplyQty;
        TempRecipeLine.Hours := RecipeLine.Hours * MultiplyQty;
        IF TempRecipeLine."Unit of Measure" = '' THEN
          TempRecipeLine."Unit of Measure" := "Estimate Line NEW"."Unit of Measure";//20-04-2010
        TempRecipeLine.INSERT;
      END; //MMA.n
    END;

    PROCEDURE CreateTempEstLine@1000000027(EstLine@1000000000 : Record 11072072);
    BEGIN
      BEGIN //MMA.n
        TempRecipeLine.INIT;
        TempRecipeLine."Estimate Line" := EstLine."Line No.";
        TempRecipeLine."Estimate No." := EstLine."Estimate No.";
        TempRecipeLine."Sub-Estimate No." := EstLine."Sub-Estimate No.";
        TempRecipeLine."Part Group" := EstLine."Part Group";
        TempRecipeLine.Part := EstLine.Part;
        TempRecipeLine."Sub Operation Code" := EstLine."Sub Operation Code";
        TempRecipeLine."Trade Item" := EstLine."Trade Item";
        TempRecipeLine."Unit of Measure" := EstLine."Unit of Measure";
        TempRecipeLine."Line Status" := EstLine."Line Status";
        TempRecipeLine.Quantity := EstLine.Quantity;
        TempRecipeLine.Norm  := EstLine.Norm;
        TempRecipeLine.Hours := EstLine.Hours;
        TempRecipeLine."Labor Cost Amount" := EstLine."Labor Cost Amount";
        TempRecipeLine."Material Cost Amount" := EstLine."Material Cost Amount";
        TempRecipeLine."Cost Object Price" := EstLine."Cost Object Price";
        TempRecipeLine."Subcontracting Cost Amount" := EstLine."Subcontracting Cost Amount";
        TempRecipeLine."Plant Cost Amount" := EstLine."Plant Cost Amount";
        TempRecipeLine."Gross Price" := EstLine."Gross Price";
        TempRecipeLine."Material Sales Amount":= EstLine."Material Sales Amount";  //GB.n
        TempRecipeLine."Subcontracting Sales Amount" := EstLine."Subcontracting Sales Amount"; //GB.n
        TempRecipeLine."Sales Amount":= EstLine."Sales Amount";
        TempRecipeLine.Description := EstLine.Description;
        //TempRecipeLine."Discount %" := EstLine."Discount %"; //MMA.n
        TempRecipeLine.INSERT;
      END; //MMA.n
    END;

    PROCEDURE FSelectAllColumns@1000000008();
    BEGIN
      PrintNorm := TRUE;
      PrintHours := TRUE;
      PrintLabor := TRUE;
      PrintBrAmnt := TRUE;
      PrintPercDisc := TRUE;
      PrintPrice := TRUE;
      PrintTotal := TRUE;
      PrintSubcontract := TRUE;
      PrintPlant := TRUE;
      PrintMaterial := TRUE;
    END;

    PROCEDURE USelectAllColumns@1000000009();
    BEGIN
      PrintNorm := FALSE;
      PrintHours := FALSE;
      PrintLabor := FALSE;
      PrintBrAmnt := FALSE;
      PrintPercDisc := FALSE;
      PrintPrice := FALSE;
      PrintTotal := FALSE;
      PrintSubcontract := FALSE;
      PrintPlant := FALSE;
      PrintMaterial := FALSE;
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckCorrFactSubEst@1000000002(Est@1000000001 : Code[20];SubEst@1000000002 : Code[20];EndLine@1000000003 : Boolean);
    VAR
      SubEstimaterRec@1000000000 : Record 11072074;
    BEGIN
      SubEstimaterRec.GET(Est,SubEst);
      IF (SubEstimaterRec."Adjustment Factor Hours" <> 1) AND (EndLine) THEN BEGIN
        CorrFactText := STRSUBSTNO(CorrTotalText,SubEstimaterRec."Adjustment Factor Hours",SubEst);
        AdjFactorHoursFact := SubEstimaterRec."Adjustment Factor Hours"; //MMA.n
      END ELSE
        IF (SubEstimaterRec."Adjustment Factor Hours" <> 1) AND NOT (EndLine) THEN BEGIN
          CorrFactText := STRSUBSTNO(CorrText,SubEstimaterRec."Adjustment Factor Hours",SubEst);
          AdjFactorHoursFact := SubEstimaterRec."Adjustment Factor Hours"; //MMA.n
        END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckCorrFactPart@1000000021(Est@1000000001 : Code[20];SubEst@1000000002 : Code[20];PartGroup@1000000004 : Code[20];Part@1000000003 : Code[20]);
    VAR
      SubEstimaterPartRec@1000000000 : Record 11072073;
    BEGIN
      SubEstimaterPartRec.GET(Est,SubEst,PartGroup,Part);
      IF SubEstimaterPartRec."Adjustment Factor Hours" <> 1 THEN BEGIN
        CorrFactPartText := STRSUBSTNO('Corectiefactor uren %1 % op onderdeel %2',SubEstimaterPartRec."Adjustment Factor Hours",Part);
        AdjFactorHours := SubEstimaterPartRec."Adjustment Factor Hours";
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE InsertNormDiffLine@1000000000(Estline@1000000000 : Record 11072072);
    BEGIN
      IF NOT ShowNormSet THEN
        EXIT;
      IF (Estline.Quantity <> 0) AND (Estline."Sub Operation Code" <> '') OR
       (Estline.Quantity <> 0) AND (Estline."Norm Group" <> '') THEN BEGIN
        TempNormDiffLine := Estline;
        TempNormDiffLine.INSERT;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE InsertNormDiffRecLine@1000000012(RecLine@1000000000 : Record 11072075);
    BEGIN
      IF NOT ShowNormSet THEN
        EXIT;

      IF (RecLine.Quantity <> 0) AND (RecLine."Sub Operation Code" <> '') OR
        (RecLine.Quantity <> 0) AND (RecLine."Norm Group" <> '')  THEN BEGIN
        TempNormDiffRecLine := RecLine;
        TempNormDiffRecLine.INSERT;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE GenerateTempLines@1000000003(EstimateNo@1000000000 : Code[20]);
    VAR
      SubEstimate@1000000001 : Record 11072074;
      SubEstimatePart@1000000002 : Record 11072073;
    BEGIN
      CLEAR(TempSubEstimateRec);
      TempSubEstimateRec.RESET;
      TempSubEstimateRec.DELETEALL;
      CLEAR(TempSubEstimatePartRec);
      TempSubEstimatePartRec.RESET;
      TempSubEstimatePartRec.DELETEALL;

      SubEstimate.SETRANGE("Estimate No.",EstimateNo);
      IF SubEstimate.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          SubEstimatePart.SETRANGE("Estimate No.",EstimateNo);
          SubEstimatePart.SETRANGE("Sub-Estimate No.",SubEstimate."Sub-Estimate No.");
          IF SubEstimatePart.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
            REPEAT
              TempSubEstimatePartRec := SubEstimatePart;
              TempSubEstimatePartRec.INSERT;
            UNTIL SubEstimatePart.NEXT = 0;
          END;
          TempSubEstimateRec := SubEstimate;
          TempSubEstimateRec.INSERT;
        UNTIL SubEstimate.NEXT = 0;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE CALCsumm@1000000007();
    VAR
      EstimateLine@1000000000 : Record 11072072;
    BEGIN
      //Specifiek materiaal
      EstimateLine.SETRANGE("Estimate No.","Estimate Line NEW"."Estimate No.");
      IF SubEstimateFilter <> '' THEN
        EstimateLine.SETFILTER("Sub-Estimate No.",SubEstimateFilter);
      EstimateLine.SETFILTER("Line Status", 'S');
      IF EstimateLine.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          SpecMatDec[1] += EstimateLine."Material Cost Amount";
        UNTIL EstimateLine.NEXT = 0;
      END;

      //Generiek materiaal
      EstimateLine.SETFILTER("Line Status", '<>S&<>P&<>V&<>RI&<>RD&<>VB');
      IF EstimateLine.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          SpecMatDec[2] += EstimateLine."Material Cost Amount";
        UNTIL EstimateLine.NEXT = 0;
      END;


      //Onderaanneming
      EstimateLine.SETFILTER("Line Status",'<>I');
      IF EstimateLine.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          SpecMatDec[3] += EstimateLine."Subcontracting Cost Amount";
        UNTIL EstimateLine.NEXT = 0;
      END;

      //Imtech Divisie
      EstimateLine.SETFILTER("Line Status",'I');
      IF EstimateLine.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          SpecMatDec[4] += EstimateLine."Subcontracting Cost Amount";
        UNTIL EstimateLine.NEXT = 0;
      END;

      //Stelposten
      EstimateLine.SETFILTER("Line Status",'P');
      IF EstimateLine.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          SpecMatDec[5] += EstimateLine."Material Cost Amount";
        UNTIL EstimateLine.NEXT = 0;
      END;

      //Verrekenprijzen
      EstimateLine.SETFILTER("Line Status",'V');
      IF EstimateLine.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          SpecMatDec[6] += EstimateLine."Material Cost Amount";
        UNTIL EstimateLine.NEXT = 0;
      END;

      //Reis en verblijfkosten
      EstimateLine.SETFILTER("Line Status",'RI|RD|VB');
      IF EstimateLine.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          SpecMatDec[7] += EstimateLine."Material Cost Amount";
        UNTIL EstimateLine.NEXT = 0;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE InsertOrModifyRates@1000000005(RateCode@1000000000 : Code[20];Hours@1000000001 : Decimal;Amount@1000000002 : Decimal);
    BEGIN
      //Project No.,Adjustment,Extension Contract,Option,Line No.
      TempEstimateRate.RESET;
      IF TempEstimateRate.GET("Estimate Line NEW"."Estimate No.", RateCode,'','',0) THEN BEGIN
        TempEstimateRate.Hours += Hours;
        TempEstimateRate.Amount += Amount;
        TempEstimateRate.MODIFY;
      END ELSE BEGIN
        TempEstimateRate."Project No." := "Estimate Line NEW"."Estimate No.";
        TempEstimateRate.Adjustment := RateCode;
        TempEstimateRate.Description := RateDesc(RateCode);
        TempEstimateRate.Rate := RateRate(RateCode);
        TempEstimateRate.Hours := Hours;
        TempEstimateRate.Amount := Amount;
        TempEstimateRate.INSERT;
        TempEstimateRate.RESET;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE RateDesc@1000000001(RateCode@1000000000 : Code[20]) : Text[50];
    VAR
      EstimateRateRec@1000000001 : Record 11012160;
    BEGIN
      IF EstimateRateRec.GET("Estimate Line NEW"."Estimate No.", RateCode) THEN
        EXIT(EstimateRateRec.Description);
    END;

    PROCEDURE RateRate@1000000011(RateCode@1000000001 : Code[20]) : Decimal;
    VAR
      EstimateRateRec@1000000000 : Record 11012160;
    BEGIN
      IF EstimateRateRec.GET("Estimate Line NEW"."Estimate No.", RateCode) THEN BEGIN
        CASE EstimateRateRec."Rate Type" OF
          EstimateRateRec."Rate Type"::Hours: EXIT(EstimateRateRec."Cost Rate");
          EstimateRateRec."Rate Type"::Minuts: EXIT(EstimateRateRec."Cost Rate" * (60 / EstimateRateRec."Team Size"));
        END;
      END;
    END;

    BEGIN
    {
      Basisrapport 11012165
    }
    END.
  }

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function
